# mode is used for arrays, and nested for nested field
# path -> the outer path of nesting
# filter -> filtering the inside the nested doc. Using this the first hit was slow. each nested doc is considered separate.

GET search_case_v1/_search?_source_excludes=TicketNotes.Notes
{
  "sort": [
    
    
    {
      "TicketNotes.CreatedOn.keyword": {
      
        "order": "desc",
        "mode": "min", 
        "nested": {
          "path": "TicketNotes",
          "filter":{
            "term": {"TicketNotes.CreatedBy" : "BCA.User"}
          }
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}

# post filter controls what should be returned in Hits. 
# best used with aggregation. the aggs will show other options. Read docs
GET search_box_v1/_search?_source_excludes=content
{
  "query": {
    "match": {
      "division": "PLP"
    }
  },
  "aggs": {
    "by_docName": {
      "terms": {
        "field": "docfilename.keyword",
        "size": 100
      }
    }
  },
  "post_filter": {
    "term": {
      "docfilename.keyword": "5400-DS04-405-RDS.pdf"
    }
  }
}
